  523 #define ALEX_GHC 1
  524 #define ALEX_NOPRED 1
  525 -- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
  526 -- ALEX TEMPLATE
  527 --
  528 -- This code is in the PUBLIC DOMAIN; you may copy it freely and use
  529 -- it for any purpose whatsoever.
  530 
  531 -- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
  532 -- INTERNALS and main scanner engine
  533 
  534 #ifdef ALEX_GHC
  535 #  define ILIT(n) n#
  536 #  define IBOX(n) (I# (n))
  537 #  define FAST_INT Int#
  538 -- Do not remove this comment. Required to fix CPP parsing when using GCC and a clang-compiled alex.
  539 #  if __GLASGOW_HASKELL__ > 706
  540 #    define GTE(n,m) (GHC.Exts.tagToEnum# (n >=# m))
  541 #    define EQ(n,m) (GHC.Exts.tagToEnum# (n ==# m))
  542 #  else
  543 #    define GTE(n,m) (n >=# m)
  544 #    define EQ(n,m) (n ==# m)
  545 #  endif
  546 #  define PLUS(n,m) (n +# m)
  547 #  define MINUS(n,m) (n -# m)
  548 #  define TIMES(n,m) (n *# m)
  549 #  define NEGATE(n) (negateInt# (n))
  550 #  define IF_GHC(x) (x)
  551 #else
  552 #  define ILIT(n) (n)
  553 #  define IBOX(n) (n)
  554 #  define FAST_INT Int
  555 #  define GTE(n,m) (n >= m)
  556 #  define EQ(n,m) (n == m)
  557 #  define PLUS(n,m) (n + m)
  558 #  define MINUS(n,m) (n - m)
  559 #  define TIMES(n,m) (n * m)
  560 #  define NEGATE(n) (negate (n))
  561 #  define IF_GHC(x)
  562 #endif
  563 
  564 #ifdef ALEX_GHC
  565 data AlexAddr = AlexA# Addr#
  566 -- Do not remove this comment. Required to fix CPP parsing when using GCC and a clang-compiled alex.
  567 
  568 {-# INLINE alexIndexInt16OffAddr #-}
  569 alexIndexInt16OffAddr :: AlexAddr -> Int# -> Int#
  570 alexIndexInt16OffAddr (AlexA# arr) off =
  571 #ifdef WORDS_BIGENDIAN
  572   narrow16Int# i
  573   where
  574         i    = word2Int# ((high `uncheckedShiftL#` 8#) `or#` low)
  575         high = int2Word# (ord# (indexCharOffAddr# arr (off' +# 1#)))
  576         low  = int2Word# (ord# (indexCharOffAddr# arr off'))
  577         off' = off *# 2#
  578 #else
  579 #if __GLASGOW_HASKELL__ >= 901
  580   GHC.Exts.int16ToInt#
  581 #endif
  582     (indexInt16OffAddr# arr off)
  583 #endif
  584 #else
  585 alexIndexInt16OffAddr = (Data.Array.!)
  586 #endif
  587 
  588 #ifdef ALEX_GHC
  589 {-# INLINE alexIndexInt32OffAddr #-}
  590 alexIndexInt32OffAddr :: AlexAddr -> Int# -> Int#
  591 alexIndexInt32OffAddr (AlexA# arr) off =
  592 #ifdef WORDS_BIGENDIAN
  593   narrow32Int# i
  594   where
  595    i    = word2Int# ((b3 `uncheckedShiftL#` 24#) `or#`
  596                      (b2 `uncheckedShiftL#` 16#) `or#`
  597                      (b1 `uncheckedShiftL#` 8#) `or#` b0)
  598    b3   = int2Word# (ord# (indexCharOffAddr# arr (off' +# 3#)))
  599    b2   = int2Word# (ord# (indexCharOffAddr# arr (off' +# 2#)))
  600    b1   = int2Word# (ord# (indexCharOffAddr# arr (off' +# 1#)))
  601    b0   = int2Word# (ord# (indexCharOffAddr# arr off'))
  602    off' = off *# 4#
  603 #else
  604 #if __GLASGOW_HASKELL__ >= 901
  605   GHC.Exts.int32ToInt#
  606 #endif
  607     (indexInt32OffAddr# arr off)
  608 #endif
  609 #else
  610 alexIndexInt32OffAddr = (Data.Array.!)
  611 #endif
  612 
  613 #ifdef ALEX_GHC
  614 -- GHC >= 503, unsafeAt is available from Data.Array.Base.
  615 quickIndex = unsafeAt
  616 #else
  617 quickIndex = (Data.Array.!)
  618 #endif
  619 
  620 -- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
  621 -- Main lexing routines
  622 
  623 data AlexReturn a
  624   = AlexEOF
  625   | AlexError  !AlexInput
  626   | AlexSkip   !AlexInput !Int
  627   | AlexToken  !AlexInput !Int a
  628 
  629 -- alexScan :: AlexInput -> StartCode -> AlexReturn a
  630 alexScan input__ IBOX(sc)
  631   = alexScanUser undefined input__ IBOX(sc)
  632 
  633 alexScanUser user__ input__ IBOX(sc)
  634   = case alex_scan_tkn user__ input__ ILIT(0) input__ sc AlexNone of
  635   (AlexNone, input__') ->
  636     case alexGetByte input__ of
  637       Nothing ->
  638 #ifdef ALEX_DEBUG
  639                                    Debug.Trace.trace ("End of input.") $
  640 #endif
  641                                    AlexEOF
  642       Just _ ->
  643 #ifdef ALEX_DEBUG
  644                                    Debug.Trace.trace ("Error.") $
  645 #endif
  646                                    AlexError input__'
  647 
  648   (AlexLastSkip input__'' len, _) ->
  649 #ifdef ALEX_DEBUG
  650     Debug.Trace.trace ("Skipping.") $
  651 #endif
  652     AlexSkip input__'' len
  653 
  654   (AlexLastAcc k input__''' len, _) ->
  655 #ifdef ALEX_DEBUG
  656     Debug.Trace.trace ("Accept.") $
  657 #endif
  658     AlexToken input__''' len ((Data.Array.!) alex_actions k)
  659 
  660 
  661 -- Push the input through the DFA, remembering the most recent accepting
  662 -- state it encountered.
  663 
  664 alex_scan_tkn user__ orig_input len input__ s last_acc =
  665   input__ `seq` -- strict in the input
  666   let
  667   new_acc = (check_accs (alex_accept `quickIndex` IBOX(s)))
  668   in
  669   new_acc `seq`
  670   case alexGetByte input__ of
  671      Nothing -> (new_acc, input__)
  672      Just (c, new_input) ->
  673 #ifdef ALEX_DEBUG
  674       Debug.Trace.trace ("State: " ++ show IBOX(s) ++ ", char: " ++ show c ++ " " ++ (show . chr . fromIntegral) c) $
  675 #endif
  676       case fromIntegral c of { IBOX(ord_c) ->
  677         let
  678                 base   = alexIndexInt32OffAddr alex_base s
  679                 offset = PLUS(base,ord_c)
  680 
  681                 new_s = if GTE(offset,ILIT(0))
  682                           && let check  = alexIndexInt16OffAddr alex_check offset
  683                              in  EQ(check,ord_c)
  684                           then alexIndexInt16OffAddr alex_table offset
  685                           else alexIndexInt16OffAddr alex_deflt s
  686         in
  687         case new_s of
  688             ILIT(-1) -> (new_acc, input__)
  689                 -- on an error, we want to keep the input *before* the
  690                 -- character that failed, not after.
  691             _ -> alex_scan_tkn user__ orig_input
  692 #ifdef ALEX_LATIN1
  693                    PLUS(len,ILIT(1))
  694                    -- issue 119: in the latin1 encoding, *each* byte is one character
  695 #else
  696                    (if c < 0x80 || c >= 0xC0 then PLUS(len,ILIT(1)) else len)
  697                    -- note that the length is increased ONLY if this is the 1st byte in a char encoding)
  698 #endif
  699                    new_input new_s new_acc
  700       }
  701   where
  702         check_accs (AlexAccNone) = last_acc
  703         check_accs (AlexAcc a  ) = AlexLastAcc a input__ IBOX(len)
  704         check_accs (AlexAccSkip) = AlexLastSkip  input__ IBOX(len)
  705 #ifndef ALEX_NOPRED
  706         check_accs (AlexAccPred a predx rest)
  707            | predx user__ orig_input IBOX(len) input__
  708            = AlexLastAcc a input__ IBOX(len)
  709            | otherwise
  710            = check_accs rest
  711         check_accs (AlexAccSkipPred predx rest)
  712            | predx user__ orig_input IBOX(len) input__
  713            = AlexLastSkip input__ IBOX(len)
  714            | otherwise
  715            = check_accs rest
  716 #endif
  717 
  718 data AlexLastAcc
  719   = AlexNone
  720   | AlexLastAcc !Int !AlexInput !Int
  721   | AlexLastSkip     !AlexInput !Int
  722 
  723 data AlexAcc user
  724   = AlexAccNone
  725   | AlexAcc Int
  726   | AlexAccSkip
  727 #ifndef ALEX_NOPRED
  728   | AlexAccPred Int (AlexAccPred user) (AlexAcc user)
  729   | AlexAccSkipPred (AlexAccPred user) (AlexAcc user)
  730 
  731 type AlexAccPred user = user -> AlexInput -> Int -> AlexInput -> Bool
  732 
  733 -- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
  734 -- Predicates on a rule
  735 
  736 alexAndPred p1 p2 user__ in1 len in2
  737   = p1 user__ in1 len in2 && p2 user__ in1 len in2
  738 
  739 --alexPrevCharIsPred :: Char -> AlexAccPred _
  740 alexPrevCharIs c _ input__ _ _ = c == alexInputPrevChar input__
  741 
  742 alexPrevCharMatches f _ input__ _ _ = f (alexInputPrevChar input__)
  743 
  744 --alexPrevCharIsOneOfPred :: Array Char Bool -> AlexAccPred _
  745 alexPrevCharIsOneOf arr _ input__ _ _ = arr Data.Array.! alexInputPrevChar input__
  746 
  747 --alexRightContext :: Int -> AlexAccPred _
  748 alexRightContext IBOX(sc) user__ _ _ input__ =
  749      case alex_scan_tkn user__ input__ ILIT(0) input__ sc AlexNone of
  750           (AlexNone, _) -> False
  751           _ -> True
  752         -- TODO: there's no need to find the longest
  753         -- match when checking the right context, just
  754         -- the first match will do.
  755 #endif
  756 {-# LINE 135 "saw-script/src/SAWScript/Lexer.x" #-}
  757 -- token helpers
  758 
  759 type Action = Pos -> Text -> LexS -> ([Token Pos], LexS)
  760 plain ::                   (Pos -> Text -> Token Pos)   -> Action
  761 xform :: (Text -> Text) -> (Pos -> Text -> Token Pos)   -> Action
  762 addon :: (Text -> a) -> (Pos -> Text -> a -> Token Pos) -> Action
  763 lexFail :: Text -> Action
  764 
  765 addToComment, startComment, endComment :: Action
  766 addToCode, startCode, endCode :: Action
  767 addToString, startString, endString :: Action
  768 addToCType, startCType, endCType :: Action
  769 
  770 plain   tok pos txt = \s -> ([tok pos txt], s)         -- ^ just the contents
  771 xform f tok pos txt = \s -> ([tok pos (f txt)], s)     -- ^ transform contents
  772 addon f tok pos txt = \s -> ([tok pos txt (f txt)], s) -- ^ also variant contents
  773 lexFail msg pos txt = \_ -> ([], LexFailed msg pos txt)
  774 
  775 startComment p txt s = ([], InComment p stack chunks done')
  776   where (stack, chunks, done') = case s of
  777           Normal                 -> ([], [txt], Normal)
  778           InComment q qs cs done -> (q : qs, txt : cs, done)
  779           InCode q ctxt          -> ([], [txt], InCode q ctxt)
  780           InCType q ctxt         -> ([], [txt], InCType q ctxt)
  781           _                      -> panic "[Lexer] startComment" ["not in normal or cryptol block or comment"]
  782 
  783 endComment _p txt s =
  784   case s of
  785     InComment f [] cs done     -> ([], addWhitespace f (Text.concat (reverse cs) <> txt) done)
  786     InComment _ (q:qs) cs done -> ([], InComment q qs (txt : cs) done)
  787     _                          -> panic "[Lexer] endComment" ["outside comment"]
  788 
  789 addToComment _ txt s = ([], InComment p stack (txt : chunks) done')
  790   where
  791   (p, stack, chunks, done') =
  792      case s of
  793        InComment q qs cs done -> (q,qs,cs,done)
  794        _                   -> panic "[Lexer] addToComment" ["outside comment"]
  795 
  796 startLineComment p txt s = ([], InLineComment p txt s)
  797 
  798 endLineComment p txt s =
  799   case s of
  800     InLineComment _f cs done -> ([], addWhitespace p (cs <> txt) done)
  801     _                    -> panic "[Lexer] endLineComment" ["outside line comment"]
  802 
  803 -- Cryptol is indentation-sensitive. Just deleting the comments could produce
  804 -- unparsable Cryptol , so we replace the removed comments with matching
  805 -- whitespace
  806 addWhitespace p txt s@(InCode _q _x) = snd $ addToCode p (whiteout txt) s
  807 addWhitespace p txt s@(InCType _q _x) = snd $ addToCType p (whiteout txt) s
  808 addWhitespace _ _ s = s
  809 
  810 whiteout = Text.map (\c -> if c == '\n' then '\n' else ' ')
  811 
  812 startString p txt s = ([],InString p txt s)
  813 
  814 endString pe txt s = case s of
  815   InString ps str done -> ([mkToken ps str], done)
  816   _               -> panic "[Lexer] endString" ["outside string"]
  817   where
  818   mkToken ps str = TLit (spanPos ps pe) (read' $ str `Text.append` txt)
  819 
  820 addToString _ txt s = case s of
  821   InString p str done -> ([],InString p (str `Text.append` txt) done)
  822   _              -> panic "[Lexer] addToString" ["outside string"]
  823 
  824 startCode p _ _ = ([],InCode p Text.empty)
  825 
  826 endCode pe _ s = case s of
  827   InCode ps str -> ([TCode (spanPos ps pe) str], Normal)
  828   _               -> panic "[Lexer] endCode" ["outside code"]
  829 
  830 addToCode _ txt s = case s of
  831   InCode p str -> ([],InCode p (str `Text.append` txt))
  832   _              -> panic "[Lexer] addToCode" ["outside code"]
  833 
  834 startCType p _ _ = ([],InCType p Text.empty)
  835 
  836 endCType pe _ s = case s of
  837   InCType ps str -> ([TCType (spanPos ps pe) str], Normal)
  838   _               -> panic "[Lexer] endCType" ["outside ctype"]
  839 
  840 addToCType _ txt s = case s of
  841   InCType p str -> ([],InCType p (str `Text.append` txt))
  842   _              -> panic "[Lexer] addToCType" ["outside ctype"]
  843 
  844 -- fetch a value via Read
  845 --
  846 -- XXX: we should not use this for string literals, because as much as
  847 -- it's convenient to have the stdlib decode escape sequences for us,
  848 -- the escape sequences available in SAWScript strings should properly
  849 -- be defined by SAWScript (that is, explicitly here) and not by
  850 -- what's in GHC's standard library.
  851 --
  852 -- FUTURE: it would be nice to get the source position into the panic
  853 -- message in case it ever actually happens, but that seems difficult
  854 -- to arrange.
  855 read' :: Read a => Text -> a
  856 read' txt = case readMaybe txt' of
  857     Just x -> x
  858     Nothing -> panic "Lexer" ["Failed to decode string or number literal", txt]
  859   where txt' = Text.unpack txt
  860 
  861 -- read a binary integer
  862 readBin :: Text -> Integer
  863 readBin s = case readInt 2 isDigit cvt (Text.unpack s') of
  864               [(a, "")] -> a
  865               _         -> panic "Lexer" ["Cannot read a binary number from: ", s]
  866   where cvt c = ord c - ord '0'
  867         isDigit c = c == '0' || c == '1'
  868         s' | "0b" `Text.isPrefixOf` s = Text.drop 2 s
  869            | "0B" `Text.isPrefixOf` s = Text.drop 2 s
  870            | True                     = s
  871 
  872 
  873 -- alex support and lexer mechanism
  874 
  875 -- current position
  876 data AlexPos = AlexPos {
  877     apLine :: !Int,
  878     apCol :: !Int
  879   }
  880 
  881 -- input state
  882 type AlexInput = (
  883     AlexPos,    -- ^ Current position
  884     Text        -- ^ Remaining input
  885   )
  886 
  887 data LexS
  888   = Normal
  889   | InComment !Pos ![Pos] [Text] LexS
  890   | InLineComment !Pos Text LexS
  891   | InString !Pos Text LexS
  892   | InCode   !Pos Text
  893   | InCType  !Pos Text
  894   | LexFailed Text !Pos Text
  895   deriving (Show)
  896 
  897 stateToInt Normal = 0
  898 stateToInt (InComment {}) = comment
  899 stateToInt (InLineComment {}) = linecomment
  900 stateToInt (InString {}) = string
  901 stateToInt (InCode {}) = code
  902 stateToInt (InCType {}) = ctype
  903 stateToInt (LexFailed msg pos _) = panic "stateToInt"
  904   [ "called on lex failure state, message"
  905   , Text.pack $ show msg
  906   , "position"
  907   , Text.pack $ show pos
  908   ]
  909 
  910 -- initial position
  911 initialPos :: AlexPos
  912 initialPos = AlexPos { apLine = 1, apCol = 1 }
  913 
  914 -- feed alex a byte describing the current char
  915 -- this came from Cryptol's lexer, which came from LexerUtils, which
  916 -- adapted the technique used in GHC's lexer.
  917 --
  918 -- FUTURE: it would be nice to share this with the saw-core lexer
  919 -- (and maybe also the Cryptol lexer) instead of pasting it repeatedly
  920 byteForChar :: Char -> Word8
  921 byteForChar c
  922   | c <= '\7' = non_graphic
  923   | Char.isAscii c = fromIntegral (ord c)
  924   | otherwise = case Char.generalCategory c of
  925       Char.LowercaseLetter       -> lower
  926       Char.OtherLetter           -> lower
  927       Char.UppercaseLetter       -> upper
  928       Char.TitlecaseLetter       -> upper
  929       Char.DecimalNumber         -> digit
  930       Char.OtherNumber           -> digit
  931       Char.ConnectorPunctuation  -> symbol
  932       Char.DashPunctuation       -> symbol
  933       Char.OtherPunctuation      -> symbol
  934       Char.MathSymbol            -> symbol
  935       Char.CurrencySymbol        -> symbol
  936       Char.ModifierSymbol        -> symbol
  937       Char.OtherSymbol           -> symbol
  938       Char.Space                 -> sp
  939       Char.ModifierLetter        -> other
  940       Char.NonSpacingMark        -> other
  941       Char.SpacingCombiningMark  -> other
  942       Char.EnclosingMark         -> other
  943       Char.LetterNumber          -> other
  944       Char.OpenPunctuation       -> other
  945       Char.ClosePunctuation      -> other
  946       Char.InitialQuote          -> other
  947       Char.FinalQuote            -> tick
  948       _                          -> non_graphic
  949   where
  950   -- CAUTION: these must match the $uni* values at the top of the file
  951   non_graphic     = 0
  952   upper           = 1
  953   lower           = 2
  954   digit           = 3
  955   symbol          = 4
  956   sp              = 5
  957   other           = 6
  958   tick            = 7
  959 
  960 -- input handler for alex
  961 alexGetByte :: AlexInput -> Maybe (Word8, AlexInput)
  962 alexGetByte (pos, text) = fmap doGet $ Text.uncons text
  963     where
  964       doGet (c, text') = (byteForChar c, (move c, text'))
  965       move c = case c of
  966           '\n' -> AlexPos { apLine = apLine pos + 1, apCol = 1 }
  967           _ -> pos { apCol = apCol pos + 1 }
  968 
  969 -- the lexer we're generating doesn't use this hook
  970 alexInputPrevChar :: AlexInput -> Char
  971 alexInputPrevChar _ = panic "Lexer" ["alexInputPrevChar"]
  972 
  973 -- read the text of a file, passing in the filename for use in positions
  974 -- and also the name to use for the EOF token
  975 scanTokens :: FilePath -> Text -> Text -> LexResult
  976 scanTokens filename eofName str0 = go (initialPos, str0) Normal
  977   where
  978     fillPos pos height width =
  979         let startLine = apLine pos
  980             startCol = apCol pos
  981             endLine = startLine + height
  982             endCol = startCol + width
  983         in
  984         Range filename startLine startCol endLine endCol
  985 
  986     go inp@(strPos, str) s = case alexScan inp (stateToInt s) of
  987         AlexEOF -> let strPos' = fillPos strPos 0 0
  988                        tok = [TEOF strPos' eofName]
  989                    in case s of
  990             Normal ->
  991                 Right (tok, Nothing)
  992             InLineComment _beginPos _ _ ->
  993                 Right (tok, Just (Warn, strPos', "Missing newline at end of file"))
  994             InComment beginPos _ _ _ ->
  995                 Left (Error, beginPos, "Unclosed block comment")
  996             InString beginPos _ _ ->
  997                 Left (Error, beginPos, "Unterminated string")
  998             InCode beginPos _ ->
  999                 Left (Error, beginPos, "Unclosed Cryptol block")
 1000             InCType beginPos _ ->
 1001                 Left (Error, beginPos, "Unclosed Cryptol type block")
 1002             LexFailed msg failPos _ -> -- should never happen, but this is its semantics anyway
 1003                 Left (Error, failPos, msg)
 1004         AlexError (failPos, _) ->
 1005             let line' = Text.pack $ show $ apLine failPos
 1006                 col' = Text.pack $ show $ apCol failPos
 1007             in
 1008             panic "Lexer" [line' <> ":" <> col' <> ": no possible token matched"]
 1009         AlexSkip inp' _len ->
 1010             go inp' s
 1011         AlexToken inp' len act ->
 1012             let text = Text.take len str
 1013                 (height, width) = case reverse $ Text.lines text of
 1014                     [] -> (0, 0)
 1015                     [line] -> (0, Text.length line)
 1016                     last_ : rest -> (length rest, Text.length last_)
 1017                 strPos' = fillPos strPos height width
 1018             in
 1019             case act strPos' text s of
 1020               (_t, LexFailed msg failPos _rest) -> Left (Error, failPos, msg)
 1021               (t, s') -> case go inp' s' of
 1022                 Left x -> Left x
 1023                 Right (ts, mmsg) -> Right (t ++ ts, mmsg)
 1024 
 1025 -- | Type to hold a diagnostic message (error or warning).
 1026 --
 1027 -- This should cease to be needed once we clean out the message
 1028 -- printing infrastructure. It's here only to shorten the type
 1029 -- signatures below, and represents the possibility of having
 1030 -- generated a message.
 1031 type DiagMsg = (Verbosity, Pos, Text)
 1032 type OptMsg = Maybe DiagMsg
 1033 type LexResult = Either DiagMsg ([Token Pos], OptMsg)
 1034 
 1035 -- entry point
 1036 lexSAW :: FilePath -> Text -> Text -> LexResult
 1037 lexSAW f eofName text = scanTokens f eofName text
